#id = 132030-39		ファシストインドと英国の関係イベント
#id = 132040-69		枢軸同盟処理イベント
#id = 132070-89		戦前外交系史実イベント
#id = 132090-109	中欧イベント
#id = 132130-219	枢軸の崩壊関連イベント
#id = 132220-39		フィンランド関連イベント
#id = 132240-59		イベリア半島関連イベント
#id = 132260-69		中東イベント
#id = 132270-77		戦後枢軸国指導者関連イベント
#id = 132278-79		アゾレス諸島要求イベント

#	中南米国家の連合国参加
#########################################################################
event = {
	id = 132000
	country = PAN
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				war = { country = USA country = GER }
				NOT = { war = { country = -1 country = GER } }
			}
			AND = {
				war = { country = USA country = JAP }
				NOT = { war = { country = -1 country = JAP } }
			}
		}
		alliance = { country = ENG country = USA }
		NOT = {
			war = { country = -1 country = USA }
			war = { country = -1 country = ENG }
			war = { country = -1 country = SOV }
		}
	}
	
	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }
	
	picture = "roosevelt"
	style = 0
	
	name = "EVT_132000_NAME"	#連合のパナマ共和国
	desc = "EVT_132000_DESC"	#
	
	action = { 
		name = "EVT_132000_ACTA"	#連合国として戦う！
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = alliance which = ENG }
		command = { type = relation which = ENG value = 80 }
		command = { type = relation which = USA value = 80 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
	}
	action = {
		name = "EVT_132000_ACTB"	#連合国とは距離を置け
		ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = dissent value = 10 }
		command = { type = domestic which = interventionism value = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 132040
	random = no
	country = SWE

	trigger = {
		atwar = no
		control = { province = 107 data = GER } #Oslo
		control = { province = 142 data = SOV } #Helsinki
		NOT = {
			exists = NOR
			exists = FIN
		}
		NOT = {
			alliance = { country = GER country = SWE }
			alliance = { country = SOV country = SWE }
			alliance = { country = ENG country = SWE }
			alliance = { country = SOV country = GER }
			war = { country = GER country = SWE }
			war = { country = GER country = SOV } #no war means sweden wont join axis and end up fighting allies too (at least not right away)
		}
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = september year = 1939 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132040_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132040_DESC"
	picture = "finish_soldiers"

	action_a = {
		ai_chance = 99
		name = "EVT_132040_ACTA"

event = {
	id = 132182
	random = no
	country = HUN

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = HUN country = SOV }
			war = { country = HUN country = USA }
			war = { country = HUN country = ENG }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			event = 131303
			event = 131304
			event = 130202
			event = 130212
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
		}
		participant = { country = -1 value = 2 }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132182_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132182_DESC"

        picture = "constitutional"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_132182_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100

#  Romania Gives Up - Germany defeated
##########
event = {
	id = 132184
	random = no
	country = ROM

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = ROM country = SOV }
			war = { country = ROM country = USA }
			war = { country = ROM country = ENG }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			event = 131303
			event = 131304
			event = 130202
			event = 130212
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
		}
		participant = { country = -1 value = 2 }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132184_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132184_DESC"

        picture = "constitutional"

		name = "EVT_132184_ACTA"

event = {
	id = 132186
	random = no
	country = BUL

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = BUL country = SOV }
			war = { country = BUL country = USA }
			war = { country = BUL country = ENG }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			event = 131303
			event = 131304
			event = 130202
			event = 130212
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
		}
		participant = { country = -1 value = 2 }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132186_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132186_DESC"

        picture = "constitutional"

	action_a = {

##########
#  Finland Gives Up - Germany defeated
##########
event = {
	id = 132188
	random = no
	country = FIN

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = FIN country = SOV }
			war = { country = FIN country = USA }
			war = { country = FIN country = ENG }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			event = 131303
			event = 131304
			event = 130202
			event = 130212
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
		}
		participant = { country = -1 value = 2 }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132188_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132188_DESC"

        picture = "constitutional"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_132188_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = leave_alliance }
		command = { type = peace which = ENG value = 1 }
		command = { type = peace which = USA value = 1 }
		command = { type = peace which = CAN value = 1 }

event = {
	id = 132194
	random = no
	country = SPR

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			war = { country = SPR country = SOV }
			war = { country = SPR country = USA }
			war = { country = SPR country = ENG }
		}
		OR = { #these signal german defeat
			event = 131301
			event = 131302
			event = 131303
			event = 131304
			event = 130202
			event = 130212
		}
		NOT = {
			war = { country = USA country = SOV }
		}
		participant = { country = -1 value = 2 }
	}

	date = { day = 0 month = january year = 1935 }
	offset = 2
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132194_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132194_DESC"

        picture = "constitutional"

			}
			AND = {
				control = { province = 341 data = VIC } #madrid
				alliance = { country = GER country = VIC }
			}
			AND = {
				control = { province = 341 data = ITA } #madrid
				alliance = { country = GER country = ITA }
			}
		}
		OR = {
			lost_VP = { country = SPA value = 50 } 
			lost_national = { country = SPA value = 50 } 
			lost_IC = { country = SPA value = 50 }
		} 
		war = { country = SPA country = GER }
	}

	random = no 
	country = GER

	trigger = {
		event = 132242 #spain gave colonies
		NOT = {
			ispuppet = SPA
		}
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 3
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132243_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132243_DESC"
	picture = "furios_hitler"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_132243_ACTA"
		ai_chance = 100
		command = { type = make_puppet which = SPA }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 132244
	random = no
	country = GER

	trigger = {
		OR = { 
			AND = { #FEPK #1.078 #スペインが消滅している
				NOT = {
					exists = SPA
					exists = SPR
				}
				OR = {
					control = { province = 341 data = GER } #madrid
					AND = {
						control = { province = 341 data = POR } #madrid
						alliance = { country = GER country = POR }
					}
					AND = {
						control = { province = 341 data = VIC } #madrid
						alliance = { country = GER country = VIC }
					}
					AND = {
						control = { province = 341 data = ITA } #madrid
						alliance = { country = GER country = ITA }
					}
				}
			}
			AND = { #スペインが降伏している
				OR = { #FEPK #1.06
					event = 132242 #spain gave colonies
					event = 60654 #spain decides to give up

				}
				OR = { #FEPK #1.06
					puppet = { country = SPA country = GER } #spain is a german puppet
					puppet = { country = SPR country = GER } #spain is a german puppet
				}
			}
		}
		alliance = { country = GER country = VIC }
	}

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 5
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1963 }

	name = "EVT_132244_NAME"
	desc = "EVT_132244_DESC"

	picture = "furios_hitler"

	action_a = {
		name = "EVT_132244_ACTA"
		#To Vichy
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 972 } #
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 971 } #
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 967 } #
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 957 } #
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 955 } #
		command = { type = secedeprovince which = VIC value = 954 } #
	}
}
